 <p data-pid="6GOUyyim">一只贩卖壁纸的鹿</p>
 <p data-pid="BrOvibVC">山川湖泊</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="J1xCYrFm">夏天有梅子味的晚霞，</p>
 <p data-pid="kchmj4-t">三两颗啤酒味的星，</p>
 <p data-pid="tPbNDoNN">以及一勺浓郁的风，</p>
 <p data-pid="wHsIgdNJ">冲开少女草莓味的心事。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="57YQ-25C">心态变老的一个明显信号，</p>
 <p data-pid="TCcUh2r_">就是“触动感”的消失。</p>
 <p data-pid="5MAa-jAW">从对微小事物的极度关切，</p>
 <p data-pid="aSG0HZIz">如草木，溪流，雨雪。</p>
 <p data-pid="eAQgv7bW">到开始执于人际，自身，道理，</p>
 <p data-pid="kU6EMrah">整个感官日渐免疫。</p>
 <p data-pid="hIRUtCdh">这种“老却”往往不是时间带来的，</p>
 <p data-pid="NhRTGV1d">而是人对自己的割裂。</p>
 <p data-pid="k-9WayoV">很喜欢vice的标语，</p>
 <p data-pid="Rjl7Xk34">叫：</p>
 <p data-pid="tdNGemCj">“世界在下沉，我们在狂欢”。</p>
 <p data-pid="4HFc6GcL">狂欢不足谈，</p>
 <p data-pid="kiJuixZe">但一定要保住“触动感”。<br><br><br></p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mfLdkyzY">我永远热爱做梦，</p>
 <p data-pid="3HjZMgpX">热爱超脱于荆棘生活之上的</p>
 <p data-pid="IaXtHY7l">一切光辉灿烂。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-a7a89f8a8b58545e101cfc38aa175b73_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="720" data-rawheight="1558" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-a7a89f8a8b58545e101cfc38aa175b73" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-7aacc7c2a42724cbd37a3681cda2becc_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="720" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-a7a89f8a8b58545e101cfc38aa175b73_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-2eaff280d8bf493b917be74eb96e4385_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="720" data-rawheight="1440" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-2eaff280d8bf493b917be74eb96e4385" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-0fa47c8081be16cc14ec9a53e4c7525a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="720" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-2eaff280d8bf493b917be74eb96e4385_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-f929f5ab90313ce25e1252dc84844cac_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="720" data-rawheight="1280" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-f929f5ab90313ce25e1252dc84844cac" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-5b241055a7d46c36301de83913e5e347_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="720" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-f929f5ab90313ce25e1252dc84844cac_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-41a43902cf0a82fd519a5a0fd481371b_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="720" data-rawheight="1280" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-41a43902cf0a82fd519a5a0fd481371b" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-bbc2759234fd5584418d94172aa3db55_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="720" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-41a43902cf0a82fd519a5a0fd481371b_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5IGpubTM">除了温柔，</p>
 <p data-pid="LBGW0c-2">同样能吸引我的特质，</p>
 <p data-pid="6yYXFk_V">还有「稳重」。</p>
 <p data-pid="EE5AqOhY">这种稳重，</p>
 <p data-pid="JWEFwbkg">无关是阅历，心态，</p>
 <p data-pid="bYHJtui4">还是知识素养带来的，</p>
 <p data-pid="U8xlXBlg">都令我痴迷。</p>
 <p data-pid="KozdLG5w">那种骨子里的从容，</p>
 <p data-pid="NCpMHuHF">不把情绪挂在脸上，</p>
 <p data-pid="ROFxjWON">处事时的沉毅，</p>
 <p data-pid="taQaHxao">是我永远都企及的状态。</p>
 <p data-pid="DE_QH_G9">生活总是那么淘气，</p>
 <p data-pid="nUsLEK2F">冗长又难捱，</p>
 <p data-pid="j8ALLhID">烦躁散尽还复来。而稳重的人，</p>
 <p data-pid="TXd3LHnW">必须要独领一份可爱。</p>
 <p data-pid="2hR-obvC">（crush～）</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="N6GLXAZP">希望你别是风</p>
 <p data-pid="xtxf149L">在我这里掀起了万般波澜</p>
 <p data-pid="N8EnyjQ5">却又跟着云去了远方</p>

 <p data-pid="mPY4D1_r">我抓不住这世间的美好</p>
 <p data-pid="y1B_SEO2">所以只能装作万事顺遂的模样</p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="OVlXVa9d">很多时候不是两个人的感情出问题了，</p>
 <p data-pid="uOkqoY1L">而是我们喜欢和自己的情绪闹别扭罢了</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="9AW3gVxr">想起张爱玲的一句话，</p>
 <p data-pid="nEEGnGEd">不相爱的爱情永久不会变坏，</p>
 <p data-pid="s3JkU-7A">所以我们只暧昧，</p>
 <p data-pid="QYq47ZIS">只调情，</p>
 <p data-pid="pboJhUve">却不要相爱</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <p data-pid="QU9QdzO0">明天再继续喜欢你吧，</p>
 <p data-pid="PI4YHujD">现在我太困了</p>

 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="lh1sjS2c">我们要有最朴素的生活，</p>
 <p data-pid="ZhfeoWbr">与最遥远的梦想 。</p>
 <p data-pid="Y3SX_fGn">即使明日天寒地冻，路远马亡。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zE8M2ha-">——七堇年</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="q7kYm-7u">望眉目有山河，</p>
 <p data-pid="xC1Kxb18">清澈明朗。</p>
 <p data-pid="cOfOuIpm">愿心中有丘壑，</p>
 <p data-pid="zwbGq6nM">一往无前。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="I-hC3gzq">我不知道将要去何方，</p>
 <p data-pid="2SPtfASl">但我已在路上。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8rg8xVWC">——宫崎骏</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="EvF-Zg-y">这个世界上有六十几亿人，</p>
 <p data-pid="LexaqMuE">但在某个瞬间，</p>
 <p data-pid="nxSEREjg">只有这一个人，</p>
 <p data-pid="b3BsRYSD">就能敌得过千军万马，</p>
 <p data-pid="maQz2nkq">四海潮生。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vUuZogsv">——独木舟</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="5WwWKSya">在整个苍穹下，</p>
 <p data-pid="S5rFYoUQ">亿万颗星辰间，</p>
 <p data-pid="ruXxROlW">我们显得多么渺小，</p>
 <p data-pid="1JB_vCi5">可是，</p>
 <p data-pid="OVq7zS7p">渺小的我们，</p>
 <p data-pid="aBEkidWY">却能看见浩瀚的整个苍穹。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JSyOp_5n">—— 桐华</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="w4dclRpg">后来许多人问我</p>
 <p data-pid="Ei2V5azM">一个人夜晚踟蹰路上的心情，</p>
 <p data-pid="6TTq2GMJ">我想起的却不是孤单和路长，</p>
 <p data-pid="wY02G6gy">而是波澜壮阔的海和天空中闪耀的星光</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3y-VgwQk">所求皆如愿，</p>
 <p data-pid="TOmh4SCr">所行化坦途，</p>
 <p data-pid="wlJQJVGP">多喜乐，</p>
 <p data-pid="Nb9Jailt">长安宁。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="2sNyeoP1">我笑，</p>
 <p data-pid="RcMfx9Li">便面如春花，</p>
 <p data-pid="SLmRZ91L">定是能感动人的，</p>
 <p data-pid="FiPDVOEs">任他是谁。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vTi5nbNf">从卖气球的人那里，</p>
 <p data-pid="vx5EkIL_">每个孩子牵走一个心愿。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GchQlZuI">玻璃晴朗，橘子辉煌，</p>
 <p data-pid="HA7NW-WQ">一颗星星刹住了脚，</p>
 <p data-pid="n-micx5N">照亮了你我。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6j9LjnTY">曙光瘫痪在大街上，</p>
 <p data-pid="P5KTb4-p">有很多地址、名字和心事，</p>
 <p data-pid="ArcrGD2-">在邮筒里避雨，</p>
 <p data-pid="TiBaxBcC">窗户打着哈欠，</p>
 <p data-pid="oU4xSS3z">风掀起夜的一角。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <hr>
 <p data-pid="So6BTZsi">少女粉系列</p>
 <p data-pid="Da8-6pmK">夜幕垂垂地下来时，</p>
 <p data-pid="gmMQE7_7">大小船上都点起灯火。</p>
 <p data-pid="oG95c7GX">从两重玻璃里映出那辐射着的黄黄的散光，</p>
 <p data-pid="PNudD4Qj">反晕出一片朦胧的烟霭；</p>
 <p data-pid="x-f5HKh6">透过这烟霭，</p>
 <p data-pid="jBKPo4qF">在黯黯的水波里，</p>
 <p data-pid="S0X0BbmG">又逗起缕缕的明漪。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <hr>
 <p data-pid="HiaUpUwF">日系小清新系列</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="iBVhZfsd">“你离开吧，</p>
 <p data-pid="RtXDNHQo">到我们初初相遇前的那一秒。</p>
 <p data-pid="etMd0vyT">另外我也该离开，</p>
 <p data-pid="sB4ufJK2">争取在那个太阳光有点斜的课间</p>
 <p data-pid="ua00VVdl">落荒而逃。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <p data-pid="RRnXCZJD">“雷声是云朵打的呼噜，</p>
 <p data-pid="fVLX8O6H">星星跟月亮都睡了，</p>
 <p data-pid="ZPFbyDih">有人在天空照相，</p>
 <p data-pid="IKZORKun">用闪电作闪光灯。”</p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="D2usvNPE">“我是需要朋友的。</p>
 <p data-pid="9lH549rw">朋友是柔软剂，</p>
 <p data-pid="b6Pk7a2e">充电器，</p>
 <p data-pid="RWAdGjRY">是糖果巧克力。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">

  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-5c081ae2ef91522204eae53d239c5b79_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="2342" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-5c081ae2ef91522204eae53d239c5b79" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-229e63651f9fd8aae89b9b01c9146b45_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-5c081ae2ef91522204eae53d239c5b79_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="wSRe3rTa">“有点怀念去年夏天，</p>
 <p data-pid="kbuupytj">弦月之下的小城，</p>
 <p data-pid="Gi6DOFn5">江边是清冽的晚风，</p>
 <p data-pid="Jpov3iy4">有路灯明晃晃地照亮一小块空地。</p>
 <p data-pid="wJBGNlWi">衣衫贴着后背，</p>
 <p data-pid="XCoSNwp1">少年人互相抹开汗涔涔的额角，</p>
 <p data-pid="unUOfuDg">悄悄耳语，</p>
 <p data-pid="trMNy9vL">说冰粉凉糕都甜不过你。”</p>
 <p data-pid="YZdcIJ6f">（作者是四川人？）</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="n0CrTjVM">“让人最安心的还是</p>
 <p data-pid="wplE9K_Y">学生时代吃饱饭后拿着一杯冰镇的果汁</p>
 <p data-pid="YM0WterW">走回教室时天空中</p>
 <p data-pid="VfKvTxZA">渐渐落下的黄昏。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-030f8ebeb719388bde2de4cf344583a9_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="720" data-rawheight="1280" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-030f8ebeb719388bde2de4cf344583a9" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-b6afac783300ae9a338015bcfcbc5124_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="720" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-030f8ebeb719388bde2de4cf344583a9_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">

 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="JsuKz7Z_">“城市的夜空只有月亮。</p>
 <p data-pid="Tm6PEeBh">想你的时候，</p>
 <p data-pid="u3LQsFNX">把湖面的镜子敲碎，</p>
 <p data-pid="RNRXunKL">让星星一颗、</p>
 <p data-pid="nmvZy-mD">一颗浮上来。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-398c1da5f1c494824a8d6b7bfd4d07f3_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="700" data-rawheight="1244" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-398c1da5f1c494824a8d6b7bfd4d07f3" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-dc711b84dcfdcb99da91496afa724e53_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="700" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-398c1da5f1c494824a8d6b7bfd4d07f3_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">

 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="IZAqkhn0">“人生的意义是什么，</p>
 <p data-pid="uqU4_O3j">我一时回答不上来。</p>
 <p data-pid="sAyLz0FK">但是我想，</p>
 <p data-pid="nAnOFgC2">人生是由细碎的快乐</p>
 <p data-pid="Ihhto3Le">和各种各样的苦辣酸甜堆起来的吧，</p>
 <p data-pid="gzAVrB3_">什么味道都有，</p>
 <p data-pid="VmBQTZUR">甜的收藏，</p>
 <p data-pid="xcbg3_J6">苦的舍弃。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 </figure>

 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="os9PCCo6">“我把什么比作你？</p>
 <p data-pid="r4RzGGWn">你是一池捞不起的波光粼粼。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-84eb0119583f1164ab4843eb91f6bcac_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="665" data-rawheight="1182" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-84eb0119583f1164ab4843eb91f6bcac" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-7db9b3fa34ab33c5cb2d06da2a4799b5_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="665" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-84eb0119583f1164ab4843eb91f6bcac_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">

 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="pMXSGZtX">猫窝在壁炉边睡着了，</p>
 <p data-pid="ItjZiViQ">天上升起一枚月亮。</p>
 <p data-pid="OyyX8pax">这不是昨天的那枚，</p>
 <p data-pid="8Uvbkzte">昨天它是白色的，</p>
 <p data-pid="ccnZ-n1h">今天它是黄色，</p>
 <p data-pid="bCYeHQsY">梨子糖一样的黄色。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-10ef7d335a96d18943abff8cb566af8a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="1924" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-10ef7d335a96d18943abff8cb566af8a" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-d6a88510a147c03c3c3b468c46e7a568_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-10ef7d335a96d18943abff8cb566af8a_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">

 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-f5d81a7d0f1c8ee6d69795034fadba51_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="1024" data-rawheight="1820" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-f5d81a7d0f1c8ee6d69795034fadba51" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-16b7de6a192c010347d0c95afa109d10_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1024" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f5d81a7d0f1c8ee6d69795034fadba51_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="jbhSjKVm">“教室里音响的嗡嗡声，</p>
 <p data-pid="Lq1r0MIX">才不是线圈的错，</p>
 <p data-pid="olG3Hxrg">一定是两个互相偷偷喜欢的人</p>
 <p data-pid="0pSjnkbJ">发送的电波相遇啦。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-8cf1ba712d28711a349922cbdae95003_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="720" data-rawheight="1281" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-8cf1ba712d28711a349922cbdae95003" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-72564b83d81b5a81394156780d586226_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="720" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-8cf1ba712d28711a349922cbdae95003_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>

  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-7af5eab80c599b9cece8a80bd57ac43a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="720" data-rawheight="1280" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-7af5eab80c599b9cece8a80bd57ac43a" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-2e6a7d37a80d2b8c03fa12421eeebf0c_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="720" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-7af5eab80c599b9cece8a80bd57ac43a_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">

 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FQ6muviO">“在广袤的空间和无限的时间中，</p>
 <p data-pid="u2IOTz3u">能与你共享同一颗行星</p>
 <p data-pid="jBruJK8u">和同一段时光是我的荣幸。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="6ssIR1q1">——卡尔·萨根</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="hmgfMZk_">“一到晴天啊，</p>
 <p data-pid="RT4JlO2G">所有的可爱就会跑出来晒太阳。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="SMXAKSlg">“幸运可能还是没有降临到我的头上，</p>
 <p data-pid="L2-PPaKu">但我相信这样心存善良地走下去，</p>
 <p data-pid="n8fjea5M">也会得到我的人生金奖券的。”</p>

 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="GaubEahX">“难过的日子，</p>
 <p data-pid="C_bNAt7a">不是挺过去的，</p>
 <p data-pid="3IEEZvHT">而是要迈过去的，</p>
 <p data-pid="trHvdT8R">是要唱着歌和不开心的事说再见的。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-6ac33bb5babc5ad943b4a752237fd679_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="627" data-rawheight="1254" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-6ac33bb5babc5ad943b4a752237fd679" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-c696dbe521f5de091a3600f2270d0e2d_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="627" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-6ac33bb5babc5ad943b4a752237fd679_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-a637d763ceab23d5f1505e91f510e1ac_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="665" data-rawheight="1182" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-a637d763ceab23d5f1505e91f510e1ac" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-567b685927f127f42313b670ef17437b_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="665" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-a637d763ceab23d5f1505e91f510e1ac_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>

 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-e736166a5e56faec0630b90323898c29_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="1918" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-e736166a5e56faec0630b90323898c29" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-25539793482dce2848132b920e499f4f_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-e736166a5e56faec0630b90323898c29_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>

  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-d57d089d5e5d2f94a8c1240f8904274a_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="458" data-rawheight="678" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-d57d089d5e5d2f94a8c1240f8904274a" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-48bfdde9688f4bd16b5a429dc760f318_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="458" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-d57d089d5e5d2f94a8c1240f8904274a_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LzdLqy5O">“我的脑袋是个小小星球，</p>
 <p data-pid="8kXlPQox">每天只有你开着月亮列车巡游。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-4a1820801405be23d7c401c9bce9a0df_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="700" data-rawheight="1244" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-4a1820801405be23d7c401c9bce9a0df" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-286c77775998908101d1b75ff6317564_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="700" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-4a1820801405be23d7c401c9bce9a0df_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-38d1d412a74fa006ff9175ab9203a3dd_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="700" data-rawheight="1245" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-38d1d412a74fa006ff9175ab9203a3dd" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-5f62ca1a0c4ba2efca3a5effb462ad89_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="700" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-38d1d412a74fa006ff9175ab9203a3dd_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="fnzxteDQ">“如果可以，</p>
 <p data-pid="SfjpbtCm">我要藏在最软最蓬的那一朵云里，</p>
 <p data-pid="tjG57qAV">悄悄探出头看着我的小朋友们</p>
 <p data-pid="0zrGKN2K">双手合十虔诚地许着那些不大不小的愿望。</p>
 <p data-pid="n0HQTVcU">我要做专属于他们的小神灵，</p>
 <p data-pid="ARtPpwu2">要认真聆听他们的每一个愿望，</p>
 <p data-pid="cCL4ICkQ">要用我微弱的灵力保佑他们万事胜意，</p>
 <p data-pid="10cPLXl9">前方云雾散尽，</p>
 <p data-pid="QdE1I9Zd">一片光明。”​</p>
 <p data-pid="GV9I8BWG">也许几亿年，</p>
 <p data-pid="MKFVq4fv">甚至几百亿年后，</p>
 <p data-pid="iPG_f1yL">我跟你都化作尘埃。</p>
 <p data-pid="wxUxxdXD">在另一个星球上遇见，</p>
 <p data-pid="g9zbj8EI">在广袤的宇宙空间里，</p>
 <p data-pid="NUTlK1GX">我们其实很近很近。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-58bf18d3f79394f26f57c703361a7c9c_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="690" data-rawheight="1227" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-58bf18d3f79394f26f57c703361a7c9c" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-73bea95bdf3c8cce29a45765beb0ace0_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="690" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-58bf18d3f79394f26f57c703361a7c9c_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-5958a46b6c1bb47cc163dbbdfc872a50_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="960" data-rawheight="1707" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-5958a46b6c1bb47cc163dbbdfc872a50" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-d9df1d47f41529a83f9756cf30c97fe3_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="960" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-5958a46b6c1bb47cc163dbbdfc872a50_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-8bd2fbf460ed96e8c622d5b225f62a04_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="960" data-rawheight="1708" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-8bd2fbf460ed96e8c622d5b225f62a04" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-4f2a5f8fcb533cb85fb109528648483b_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="960" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8bd2fbf460ed96e8c622d5b225f62a04_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-91b327ed4c76be664816633c10dd4e41_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="960" data-rawheight="1707" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-91b327ed4c76be664816633c10dd4e41" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-fab32fb9630234db586cfd75bfb9ffd7_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="960" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-91b327ed4c76be664816633c10dd4e41_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="F0btUp7n">你身体里的每一个原子都来自</p>
 <p data-pid="ysLIyHUq">一颗爆炸了的恒星，</p>
 <p data-pid="LcgF-YSC">形成你左手的原子</p>
 <p data-pid="bFsz1C0w">可能和形成你右手的来自不同的恒星。</p>
 <p data-pid="ZO7sIsFJ">这是我所知的</p>
 <p data-pid="zLUwzf0x">关于物理的最有诗意的事情：</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RwW6s14T">你们都是星尘。”</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-6affa1333e9f2338e9181912fe5450fb_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="1921" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-6affa1333e9f2338e9181912fe5450fb" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-631fd01fc4dd756852c0134604258170_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-6affa1333e9f2338e9181912fe5450fb_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-b1b463dfd6ca18b16192d1480d1e5924_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="690" data-rawheight="1227" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-b1b463dfd6ca18b16192d1480d1e5924" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-7b62824244769db6897faeb19b773e5e_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="690" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-b1b463dfd6ca18b16192d1480d1e5924_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-aa3dc65bbf2c99237affb03c55487178_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="750" data-rawheight="1334" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-aa3dc65bbf2c99237affb03c55487178" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-23524318449f1d49b9fefb2738f812d5_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="750" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-aa3dc65bbf2c99237affb03c55487178_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-9d5d69a1e839f8a972bbcc08611a7725_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="750" data-rawheight="1334" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-9d5d69a1e839f8a972bbcc08611a7725" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-7377723d9b751e21c6549853c3b9ac68_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="750" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-9d5d69a1e839f8a972bbcc08611a7725_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mlgvms_K">黑暗中我们抬头。</p>
 <p data-pid="3QZf_5gu">星辰从远方赶来，赴一面之约。</p>
 <p data-pid="Z8QYD3To">这种相遇是宇宙级别的浪漫。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-939512f800bd38a7b16ccb16b638f7d6_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="960" data-rawheight="1707" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-939512f800bd38a7b16ccb16b638f7d6" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-b621e4b26c23b29075c65f98401f00f2_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="960" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-939512f800bd38a7b16ccb16b638f7d6_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-dcd0571ac64a20510adbc713bb671a41_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="960" data-rawheight="1707" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-dcd0571ac64a20510adbc713bb671a41" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-2550a77b70f5d0ea28d65f8d3eeb9e64_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="960" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-dcd0571ac64a20510adbc713bb671a41_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-94140a51bd425d715805a7cf3d88c044_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="540" data-rawheight="960" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-94140a51bd425d715805a7cf3d88c044" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-9ca9d19ba875a4ddf78aa2aa835f0cfb_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="540" data-original="https://pica.zhimg.com/v2-94140a51bd425d715805a7cf3d88c044_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>

  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-72e6014d53b4e11cbf3ff1729d942028_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="960" data-rawheight="1707" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-72e6014d53b4e11cbf3ff1729d942028" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-4751382837880d061d1ac4328635ede8_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="960" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-72e6014d53b4e11cbf3ff1729d942028_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="tUcMN0Yp">每个人 你所热爱的一切</p>
 <p data-pid="fEIRBjM6">你所憎恨的一切</p>
 <p data-pid="2BOQHrIp">你所拥有的最宝贵的东西</p>
 <p data-pid="RP0mXha9">在宇宙生命最为伊始的几分钟内</p>
 <p data-pid="ZShKEIzV">由自然的力量合成</p>
 <p data-pid="vGyaxfgy">在恒星的中心转化</p>
 <p data-pid="vhSQrj_8">或者在他们燃烧的消亡中诞生</p>
 <p data-pid="B2Gnhors">而当你去世的时候</p>
 <p data-pid="kTbI8XH0">这些碎片将回到宇宙中</p>
 <p data-pid="Wd9bSb1h">进入无限的死亡 又重生的轮回之中</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-71d9809eea385ed8c67b609d3624a19c_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="960" data-rawheight="1706" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-71d9809eea385ed8c67b609d3624a19c" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-765b62e7a48f5db107140da1770fe502_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="960" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-71d9809eea385ed8c67b609d3624a19c_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">

 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="KWfeRdma">倘若你的眼睛这样冷，</p>
 <p data-pid="mhga_QY-">有个人的心会结成冰。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zK_L62lt">——沈从文</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="xeHkfAdN">敬万水江海，敬山峦叠翠，</p>
 <p data-pid="-dLyFRrK">拜朗朗晴空，拜璀璨星河，</p>
 <p data-pid="XmJwUwwS">此生有幸与你，</p>
 <p data-pid="LHdobQqR">躬身共戴这举世荣光。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="gK1Cwx2f">——微博</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8DHsvs4c">我心中不会有黄昏，<br>
  有你在，永远像初春的清晨。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mzXUtRxo">——《岁月》</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-a6423ea8873d45a84d5fb151715c3857_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="608" data-rawheight="1080" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-a6423ea8873d45a84d5fb151715c3857" data-default-watermark-src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-272fb04d50cf11dd163d863225232ff9_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="608" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-a6423ea8873d45a84d5fb151715c3857_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="zVqsez6a">地球正一点点的疏离月亮。</p>
 <p data-pid="LYBTK-vz">据说，</p>
 <p data-pid="ECNEAi3G">每一百万年就会陌生一秒，</p>
 <p data-pid="vMwvkEr0">早在25亿年前，</p>
 <p data-pid="Vv71Mgg6">我们便开始了漫长的别离</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pica.zhimg.com/50/v2-416d531fd13523e4cfb54f78ee089e2b_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="1920" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-416d531fd13523e4cfb54f78ee089e2b" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-10c896c90c1876d1e3c2cb52c4b60e27_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-416d531fd13523e4cfb54f78ee089e2b_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-101fb771877296fe7c9a1c061ae780c5_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="640" data-rawheight="1138" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-101fb771877296fe7c9a1c061ae780c5" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-4c5f9a2ac41c44980f991836f177b5a8_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="640" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-101fb771877296fe7c9a1c061ae780c5_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-12eb8206278b0c2b0c97324b1762ffab_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="640" data-rawheight="1138" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-12eb8206278b0c2b0c97324b1762ffab" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-814d6ad39d8c545c9544156c2c6c3fe5_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="640" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-12eb8206278b0c2b0c97324b1762ffab_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-0937271bf7f578531fdf3ae51cd4c040_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="900" data-rawheight="1600" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-0937271bf7f578531fdf3ae51cd4c040" data-default-watermark-src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-fc3a9a0afbea53ce8d2bae65f29c7c75_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="900" data-original="https://picx.zhimg.com/v2-0937271bf7f578531fdf3ae51cd4c040_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="y0eLEkj-">看到此刻的你，</p>
 <p data-pid="VPGFpGIW">一定在长吁一口气，</p>
 <p data-pid="V-hFM3aX">想象着明天又会怎样</p>
 <p data-pid="V6oq7hv3">宇宙给予我们的温柔不止于此。</p>
 <p data-pid="tEwaUG3L">被城市的霓虹衬得微弱的星光，</p>
 <p data-pid="LZ4U8EdE">可能从二百五十万年前就踏上了旅程。</p>
 <p data-pid="50nylq9E">那时地球上还没有人类，</p>
 <p data-pid="paFFiYEU">远古的祖先能人，</p>
 <p data-pid="YyRrjmgt">正在非洲广袤的平原上漫步。</p>
 <p data-pid="Vib2AbvF">就是在那些光线穿行于无垠宇宙的同时，</p>
 <p data-pid="KIEqP-Sq">人类不断进化，</p>
 <p data-pid="VrGrcuDK">一代又一代的生老病死，</p>
 <p data-pid="lJw8Og9r">周而复始。</p>
 <p data-pid="q5j1jzHH">旅途开始的二百五十万年后，</p>
 <p data-pid="bp1htp5N">这些远道而来的信使，</p>
 <p data-pid="VoBOg0uW">穿越漫长的时间，</p>
 <p data-pid="cnuaeyMb">映入现在我们的眼帘。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="ov8zJrvc">——————《我们盛装出席》</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 </figure>

 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="L9y_gSiB">倘若你的眼睛这样冷，</p>
 <p data-pid="X0QQbjmo">有个人的心会结成冰。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="UPP39r_X">——沈从文</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="3RF-lUyg">世界上最美不过的景致，<br>
  是那些最初的心动不为人知。</p>
 <p data-pid="AR1ohg2v"><br>
  ——仓央嘉措</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="qC10XMbZ">心里怀念着人，<br>
  见了泽上的萤火，<br>
  也疑是从自己身体里出来的梦游的魂。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="BsEs5L1q">——和泉式部《敕撰集》</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="94wtms0I">我把荆棘当作铺满鲜花的原野，<br>
  人间便没有什么能将我折磨。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="FxmntGq5">——张贤亮《绿化树》</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="vAcscOhg">太阳的命运也是所有恒星的命运</p>
 <p data-pid="Wv_MstYo">终有一天 它们都会消亡</p>
 <p data-pid="eqohIo85">宇宙将会陷入永无止境的黑暗之中</p>
 <p data-pid="A8F6BuIc">这便是时间镜头最深远的影响</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="97BUIu-F">岁月极美，</p>
 <p data-pid="qz3XAe5K">在于它必然的流逝。</p>
 <p data-pid="OtfGvWtd">春花、秋月、夏日、冬雪。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="i_kx5p1O">——三毛 《岁月》</p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="RFYvEBXH">你最可爱，</p>
 <p data-pid="9nUdmFgG">我说时来不及思索，</p>
 <p data-pid="YxvoLs-E">但思索之后，</p>
 <p data-pid="zs1CLiHB">还是这样说。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="_vWH_kiU">——普希金</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="0hBcG6gW">人永远都无法知道自己该要什么，</p>
 <p data-pid="Y-9DV0S7">因为人只能活一次，</p>
 <p data-pid="L4KUG-MN">既不能拿它跟前世相比，</p>
 <p data-pid="cGDjT-fT">也不能在来生加以修正。</p>
 <p data-pid="nAfMjGKu">没有任何方法可以检验哪种抉择是好的，</p>
 <p data-pid="skiVrbLW">因为不存在任何比较。</p>
 <p data-pid="BxXOKne2">一切都马上经历，</p>
 <p data-pid="iz6MfHEz">仅此一次，不能准备。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="mTD8nabG">——米兰·昆德拉</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LeiBw2GD">我永恒的灵魂，注视着你的心，</p>
 <p data-pid="Hejzxdz0">纵然黑夜孤寂，白昼如焚。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="A8J_qhTG">——兰波</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>

 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="8_5-0OrV">我的肩上是风，</p>
 <p data-pid="pLNtlgMW">风上是闪烁的星群。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="LF3xlSUC">——北岛</p>
 <p data-pid="pW1z2RoP">《结局或开始·献给遇罗克》</p>

 </figure>
 <figure data-size="normal">
  <img src="https://pic1.zhimg.com/50/v2-aae983d503e540a94bbb9c3d6d60e299_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" data-rawwidth="1080" data-rawheight="1920" data-size="normal" data-caption="" data-original-token="v2-aae983d503e540a94bbb9c3d6d60e299" data-default-watermark-src="https://picx.zhimg.com/50/v2-62065ef8b83d63dd4c9cf52dce01c6a4_720w.jpg?source=1940ef5c" class="origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb" width="1080" data-original="https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-aae983d503e540a94bbb9c3d6d60e299_r.jpg?source=1940ef5c">
 </figure>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MZD9Iy5W">一件事无论太晚或者太早，</p>
 <p data-pid="f4x-xIcJ">都不会阻拦你成为你想成为的那个人，</p>
 <p data-pid="221zMFJA">这个过程没有时间的期限，</p>
 <p data-pid="stNYVDct">只要你想，随时都可以开始。</p>
 <p data-pid="4rbb83Xn">要改变或者保留原状都无所谓，</p>
 <p data-pid="ALDhsHrC">做事本不应该有所束缚，</p>
 <p data-pid="MRv-pDGt">我们可以办好这件事却也可以把它搞砸，</p>
 <p data-pid="mk0WW6Qy">但我希望最终你能成为你想成为的人。</p>
 <p class="ztext-empty-paragraph"><br></p>
 <p data-pid="MYxkQnHu">——《返老还童》</p>
 <figure data-size="normal">
